  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_3fa8fb28-589b-4a6f-ab4a-42cbb421c606'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initializeSiwa();

              <span id="reviewTextContainer861391349" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer7726048793946066675"><blockquote>
  <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/list/4622890?shelf=na-experiment' rel='nofollow noopener'>
    <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393006047i/8646654.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  </a>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393211156i/8677119._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Oh, little crazy book, you were one <b>HUGE unexpected surprise</b>. I mean, surely the chances of enjoying two New Adult books in the space of just a couple of days is about 10 million to one? Two New Adult books that are insanely different, themes and worlds apart from one another, and yet both good? Impossible, one might think! But I was utterly mesmerised by this book that was part love story and part - and this is the bit that <b>fascinated</b> me - psychological thriller. Just before I get o</span>
  <span id="freeText7726048793946066675" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/list/4622890?shelf=na-experiment" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393006047i/8646654.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393211156i/8677119._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Oh, little crazy book, you were one <b>HUGE unexpected surprise</b>. I mean, surely the chances of enjoying two New Adult books in the space of just a couple of days is about 10 million to one? Two New Adult books that are insanely different, themes and worlds apart from one another, and yet both good? Impossible, one might think! But I was utterly mesmerised by this book that was part love story and part - and this is the bit that <b>fascinated</b> me - psychological thriller. Just before I get onto the good stuff, I feel like I should warn everyone straight away that there is a particularly graphic and disturbing rape scene that some of you may want to avoid. But if you can stomach the horrors, read onward.<br><br>At the beginning of this book, we immediately meet our protagonist, Naomi Carradine, who is in a mental institution. Naomi is adamant that she knows the truth: she is in love with Max - the man who haunts her every thought and whom she misses dearly. But no one else will believe her story. The doctors seem to think that Max isn't real, that he only exists inside Naomi's mind. Telling a story that alternates between her present life in the mental hospital and the past as she retells it to her psychiatrist, Naomi weaves a picture of her life. <b>Who is Max? Is he real, as Naomi claims him to be? Will the doctors ever believe her story? And, even more importantly, will you?</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1393206339i/8676552._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I won't claim to be the most astute reader, but I don't think I'm bad at working things out, and this book <b>kept me guessing right up until the end</b>. I had several theories as to what was going on and I didn't come near to the truth until the ending was just around the corner. I love psychological stories that explore the <b>dark aspects of the human mind</b> and keep the reader wondering where the line between fiction and reality is drawn.<br><br>There's some sexy bits in this novel, as seems to be a requirement in New Adult, which was all well and good. I have to admit that any romancing and sexy times got side-swept for me by the far more interesting psychological side to the story. While the book is quite heavy on the romance/sex, at its heart it's really about something else entirely. Which is perhaps what makes it stand out. But both Max and Lachlan were <b>sexy, sweet and completely free of douchebagitis</b> so I liked the hot lovin' parts of the book well enough. <br><br><b>
  <i>"I can dream. I can imagine and hope, but it will never change a thing. And the most terrifying thing is that I know, I know there’s more to the story. There’s another train coming straight at me, at full speed. Yet I can’t see it. I can only hear the ground slightly tremble. The tracks rattling beneath my feet. I can hear the sound of a whistle blaring. But I can’t move. All I can do is hope that when it does hit, I die in seconds."</i>
</b><br><br>My first feeling as I put this book (well, my kindle) down was that I wanted to start again from the beginning and see how everything looked from the perspective of someone who knows the truth. I love books that can do that. That surprise you. I only hope the rest of you find this as engrossing as I did.<br><br><b>
  <i>“I’m not crazy,” I repeat. “I’m not crazy. I’m not crazy…”</i>
</b> - <u>do you believe her?</u><br><br><a href="http://thebookgeek.co.uk" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.leafmarks.com/emilymay" rel="nofollow noopener">Leafmarks</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/thebookgeekreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/thebookgeek01" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="http://instagram.com/emleemay" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="http://mycountryheart.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Tumblr</a></span>

<div id="review_591039891" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/591039891" />
    <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads"><img alt="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1578074503p2/8524618.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/591039891?book_show_action=true">Apr 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads" href="/user/show/8524618-angie---angie-s-dreamy-reads">Angie - Angie&#39;s Dreamy Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer591039891" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17865553719714781459">Stringing words together to form coherent sentences after reading this is almost impossible. I keep saying this, but I have to say it again. I lost my heart somewhere in this book and it hasn't been returned to me. <br/><br/><b>It stole it. <br/>It owned it.<br/>It broke it.<br/>It unraveled it.<br/>It moved it.</b> <br/><br/>The last year I've been struggling with reading. Books have been boring me. I've stopped a ridiculous amount of them at 30% and just moved on. I've sucked at reviewing. It's gotten to the point it's pathetic. I've becom</span>
  <span id="freeText17865553719714781459" style="display:none">Stringing words together to form coherent sentences after reading this is almost impossible. I keep saying this, but I have to say it again. I lost my heart somewhere in this book and it hasn't been returned to me. <br /><br /><b>It stole it. <br />It owned it.<br />It broke it.<br />It unraveled it.<br />It moved it.</b> <br /><br />The last year I've been struggling with reading. Books have been boring me. I've stopped a ridiculous amount of them at 30% and just moved on. I've sucked at reviewing. It's gotten to the point it's pathetic. I've become a blogger that rarely reviews. It's hard to find a book that makes me want to scream it from the rooftops and I refuse to pour my heart into a review that didn't make me want to sing, dance and feel alive. I was becoming despondent, desperate for something to steal the breath from my lungs. To wrap its warm arms around me and bury itself into my deepest recesses. I wasn't sure how I'd feel about this one. <br /><br />I'm a romance reader. <br /><br />This is not your typical romance. It's a physiological thriller with romance in it. <br /><br />I didn't think it would be something I would go crazy for. I honest to God didn't. <br /><br />I was wrong!<br /><br /><b>WRONG.<br />WRONG.<br />WRONG.</b><br /><br />I'm trying desperately, searching for words to explain myself. To explain to you why you need to read this book. <br /><br />God, please, please read this book.<br /><br />It took me, swept me into its current and kept tossing me around. It burned its way into my brain, scarring it in a way that makes it deliciously unforgettable.<br /><br />The plot, well I figured it out early. About a quarter way into the book. The clues were there, blazing and bright. I don't know if the author did this on purpose. If she did, I think it was brilliant. <br /><br /><b>PURE F*CKING BRILLIANCE.</b> <br /><br />Let me explain why... <br /><br />You see, knowing what was going on made the pain in this story all the more real. It permeated my heart, surrounded me and choked the feelings from my soul. It shook me, made me bleed. <br /><br />I couldn't stop reading. <br /><br />I haven't had that feeling in so long I forgot what it actually felt like. It's euphoric, blissful, a drug which flows so thickly through your system you're in a cloudy haze that is only Lach, Lana, Naomi and Max. <br /><br />The pain ... jeeeezzzzzzz.<br /><br />I had to rub my chest, put my head between my legs to gather my breath. I had to read through eyes flowing with tears. Cheeks stained red from rubbing my face. <br /><br />I felt this book. <br /><br /><b>I FELT IT, FELT EVERY OUNCE OF MENTAL ANGUISH.</b> Every part of her trauma. The pull and push of her mind.<br /><br />I saw the unraveling of her secrets. I wanted to reach into the book and hold her to me. Comfort her and love her. I wanted to scream, fight, kick, and bleed with her. I wanted to be the balm to her ache. I wanted to save her, help her. <br /><br />This is deep.<br /><br /><b>DEEP.</b><br /><br />The characters are brilliantly shown, not told. The story unfolds like a puzzle, pulling you into its grips. It's tantalizing. It's heart wrenching. It's interesting. It's intriguing. <br /><br /><b>IT'S EVERYTHING.</b><br /><br />A perfectly and intricately crafted web of anguish. <br /><br />Lana, the broken girl, scared, hurt, troubled, wanting to be loved. But not knowing anything, but pain. <br /><br />Naomi, the strong, confident glue that holds Lana together. The beat of Lana's heart. She keeps her sane in a way. <b>AHHHHHH!</b> My lord. <br /><br />Max, the sexy, unf*ckingbelievably hot Alpha that sweeps you off your feet, that takes your heart between his palms and <b>SLAYS IT</b> from the first look, to the last.<br /><br />Lach ... Sweet Jesus, Lach. The strong, confident childhood friend that grows into the love of your life. The backbone, the healer, the man that takes you and saves you! The everything. <b>EVERYTHING.</b> #teamlach <br /><br />Mother of all that is good and holy...<br /><br /><b>WHAT CAN I SAY?</b> There's nothing. No words that can do it justice. No words that can describe what it did to my heart, soul and mind.<br /><br />This author did what the title implies. <br /><br /><b>SHE UNRAVELED ME. <br />SHE STOLE MY REALITY.<br />SHE CLIMBED INTO MY HEART.<br />SHE EMBEDDED HERSELF IN MY PORES.</b><br /><br />I'm blown away. <br /><br />You don't need to know anything more than this. It'll be a spoiler. Just read it. Feel it. <b>LOOK CLOSELY.</b> See the story behind the story. Feel the anguish. Let it take you. Let the words grip your soul. Find the healing behind the pain. <br /><br />This is more than a book. <br /><br /><b>THIS IS WHY WE READ!</b> <br /><br />Unravel is the best book of 2014 by a mile wide. To be truthful it's one of the best books I've <b>EVER</b> read! <br /><br />Wow, just <b>WOW!</b> No star rating could <b>EVER</b> be enough. <br /><br /><b>AMAZON LINK:</b> <a href="http://amzn.to/1dzUdcC" rel="nofollow noopener">http://amzn.to/1dzUdcC</a><br /><br />PS: Please be advised that this book contains rape. It is for adults only (IMO) and touches on several elements that should not be taken lightly. <br /><br /><b>
  <u>♥♥♥ FAVORITE QUOTES ♥♥♥</u>
</b><br /><br />❥<i>"F*ck the truth. It was the heart that was my worst enemy. It was the one that was going to cut me. Bleed me. It would be the one that would kill me."</i> <b>&lt;&lt;--- My soul felt this.</b> <br /><br />❥<i>"Remember that even the purest of souls have darkness in them. It might be hard to spot. Perhaps they've perfect the art of covering it from the world. Or maybe it's hidden in a dark corner of their mind. But it's there. No one in this world is scar free."</i> <b>&lt;&lt;----WHAT A QUOTE!</b><br /><br />❥<i>"Tell me what you're fighting and I'll fight with you," he whispers into my hair." </i> <b>&lt;&lt;&lt;------- MELT ME, F*CK ME, TAKE ME. I can't even. *lets out a labored breath*</b><br /><br />❥<i>"When I touch you I want you to always remember it comes from me and no one else." His fingers drift over my hips, across my inner thigh. "I want you to never forget me."</i> <b>&lt;&lt;--- OWN ME, IMPRINT YOURSELF INTO ME, LOVE ME! Whewwwwwwww **licks lips*</b><br /><br />❥<i>"I've decided that love is a sickness. But not at first. At first it's delicious. Just like a dessert. Nothing compares to that first bite. And you don't savor, but you become ravenous. You know this could be the best thing you've ever had, so you keep tasting, you keep taking. Your greed clouds reason and by the time you realize you've gone too far, it's too late. The love is gone and you're left with nothing, but pain."</i><b> &lt;&lt;&lt;----- THIS MADE ME SOB. Truth, truth, truth!</b><br /><br />❥<i>"Sex. Love. Fucking. Call it what you want but they are all the same. Each one requires you to give a piece of yourself that you can never get back. But with the right person, everything will align perfectly. The world stops turning on it's axis, time slows and you realize that while you're losing a piece of yourself, you're also gaining something in return."</i><b> &lt;&lt;&lt;------ SHIVERS. FULL BODY SHIVERS! </b><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="17865553719714781459" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_857884630" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/857884630" />
    <a title="destini mia" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia"><img alt="destini mia" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1499903277p2/13742215.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/857884630?book_show_action=true">Feb 17, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="destini mia" class="user" itemprop="url" name="destini mia" href="/user/show/13742215-destini-mia">destini mia</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13742215-destini-mia?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer857884630" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4524154468340398635"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392775951i/8609538.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><i>
  <blockquote>“God offers to every mind its choice between truth and repose. Take which you please– you can never have both.”</blockquote>
</i><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392777153i/8609732.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Brilliant.</b> <i>This book</i>... I'm still not sure what it's done to me. I was <i>
  <b>mesmerized</b>
</i> by <i>Unravel</i>. I was <i>
  <b>consumed</b>
</i> by the need to know what was going on and it was unputdownable!<br/><br/><i>
  <blockquote>“Most people believe the truth is a delicate little bird. They think it's harmless. But I know something they don't.” </blockquote>
</i><br/>____________________________________________<br/><br/><pre> ♦︎ The Story ♦︎ </pre><br/>______________________</span>
  <span id="freeText4524154468340398635" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392775951i/8609538.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>
  <blockquote>“God offers to every mind its choice between truth and repose. Take which you please– you can never have both.”</blockquote>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392777153i/8609732.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Brilliant.</b> <i>This book</i>... I'm still not sure what it's done to me. I was <i>
  <b>mesmerized</b>
</i> by <i>Unravel</i>. I was <i>
  <b>consumed</b>
</i> by the need to know what was going on and it was unputdownable!<br><br><i>
  <blockquote>“Most people believe the truth is a delicate little bird. They think it's harmless. But I know something they don't.” </blockquote>
</i><br>____________________________________________<br><br><pre> ♦︎ The Story ♦︎ </pre><br>____________________________________________<br><br><i>Six months ago, I was happy. I was simply Naomi Carradine. <br><br>One month ago, I was admitted into a psych ward. <br><br>Yesterday, Lachlan visited me. Kissed me. And told me that I’m starting to lose my mind. <br><br>Hours later, Max haunted my thoughts, reminding me I’m not crazy and that he needs my help. <br><br>A few minutes ago, I drifted further from reality, trying to unravel the past. <br><br>And now...everyone thinks I’m insane. But, I know he's real, and I know he needs me. <br><br>Do you believe me?</i><br><br>---------------------------------------------------------------------------<br><b>I had to use the Goodreads blurb. If I made my own recap I probably would have said too much. </b><br>---------------------------------------------------------------------------<br><br>This was <i>
  <b>one hell of a ride.</b>
</i> From start to finish, I couldn't tear my eyes away. I had to suffer the whole day feeling like sh*t warmed over because I used the <i>'just one more chapter'</i> line. One chapter was most definitely not enough. <br><br>I was constantly thinking up new theories, trying to get a grasp of what was going on... the <i>
  <b>unpredictability</b>
</i> of <i>Unravel</i> kept me on my toes. <br><br>I wish I could say that I <i>
  <b>savored</b>
</i> every page, <i>every</i> word and took my absolute time reading but I just couldn't. I'm <s>nosy</s> <i>
  <b>curious</b>
</i> by nature so being emerged in this <i>wtf</i> story... there was no way I could survive long without knowing <i>
  <b>everything.</b>
</i><br><i>
  <blockquote> “I’ve decided that love is a sickness. But not a first.”</blockquote>
</i><br>____________________________________________<br><br> <pre>♦︎ Characters ♦︎ </pre><br>____________________________________________<br><i>
  <blockquote> “I think we’re all trying to be a winner in a losing game.”</blockquote>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392779479i/8610272.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392779479i/8610273.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>I'll have to be really vague about the characters, as to not give anything away... </b><br>Each character was shrouded in mystery. Especially <b>Naomi.</b> I had so many thoughts running through my head– could I trust her and/or anything she's telling me, is what she's saying even true, is she crazy, or the even bigger question, is she <i>
  <b>sane</b>
</i>...?<br>____________________________________________<br><br> <pre> ♦︎ Overall ♦︎ </pre><br>____________________________________________<br><br>What really solidified the five stars for me was that, while <i>Unravel</i> dealt with some <b>weighty</b> subjects, <b>it didn't suffocate me.</b> I didn't feel like I was <i>drowning</i> in everything. I never felt like it was <i>too</i> much.<br>And despite all the <b>
  <i>uncertainty </i>
</b> and pain, this was also a story about <i>
  <b>love</b>
</i> and <i>
  <b>healing.</b>
</i><br> <br>If you're looking for a <b>
  <i>atypical</i>
</b> story with mystery and a good dose of some <b>steamy</b> scenes then look no further!<br><i>
  <blockquote>“Tell me what you’re fighting and I’ll fight with you,” he whispers into my hair. </blockquote>
</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392780279i/8610435.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="4524154468340398635" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_828730210" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/828730210" />
    <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog"><img alt="Aestas Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1353371225p2/5604583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/828730210?book_show_action=true">Jan 19, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer828730210" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14492222246465742596"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392619512i/8585079._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>*** SPOILER FREE REVIEW *** <b> 4.5 stars </b><br/><br/><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> "…everyone thinks I’m insane. But, I know he’s real, and I know he needs me. Do you believe me?" </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br/><b> Wow -- my mind is spinning!!<br/><br/><i>Unravel </i> hooked me right from the start, kept me guessing the whole way through, and both shocked and impressed me with the way all the intricately woven layers came together at the end. </b><br/><br/>I honestly feel like this is one of those books where the less you know about it, the more you'll enjoy it. Also, literally anything I </span>
  <span id="freeText14492222246465742596" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392619512i/8585079._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*** SPOILER FREE REVIEW *** <b> 4.5 stars </b><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote> "…everyone thinks I’m insane. But, I know he’s real, and I know he needs me. Do you believe me?" </blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><b> Wow -- my mind is spinning!!<br><br><i>Unravel </i> hooked me right from the start, kept me guessing the whole way through, and both shocked and impressed me with the way all the intricately woven layers came together at the end. </b><br><br>I honestly feel like this is one of those books where the less you know about it, the more you'll enjoy it. Also, literally anything I say about the storyline will either give something away or be misleading so I'm actually not going to talk about the plot at all in this review. The only thing I'll share is the book's blurb (which was all I knew going into the story too)....<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>Six months ago, I was happy. I was simply Naomi Carradine.<br><br>One month ago, I was admitted into a psych ward.<br><br>Yesterday, Lachlan visited me. Kissed me. And told me that I’m starting to lose my mind.<br><br>Hours later, Max haunted my thoughts, reminding me I’m not crazy and that he needs my help.<br><br>A few minutes ago, I drifted further from reality, trying to unravel the past.<br><br>And now...everyone thinks I’m insane. But, I know he's real, and I know he needs me.<br><br><b>Do you believe me? </b></i>
</blockquote><br><br>Like I said, I was hooked from the first chapter and was instantly drawn into the story. By the end of the second chapter, I just got these <i>chills</i> and there was just no turning back.<br><br>Here we have the story of a girl whose world was collapsing around her -- she'd been involuntarily committed to a mental health institute, the guy she counted on left her, her memories of another guy haunted her, and no one believed her. This was her story. It was told in pieces -- bits in the past, bits in the present.... some parts in her mind, some parts in reality... and it was up to you to try and figure out what was real.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Each time I see him, I become convinced that it will be different, that he won't disappear on me."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>From the beginning, the biggest questions I had were -- Was this girl crazy or sane? How much of what I was reading was real? Were these memories real? Was the present day real? Was it all in her head or was it really happening? I loved that feeling of just not knowing what to think... where literally anything was a possibility.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Every day is unknown for me. Every day I wake up feeling like I'm surrounded by a heavy fog and I know I'm missing a piece of myself, and I don't know where it is." </i>
</blockquote><br><br>I'm getting a lot of readers asking me if there is a romance and the answer is -- yes!! The romance is an integral part of the story. It's not the only part, but it's definitely a strong, central element.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"My heart is stuck in my throat, as I look him over. I love him so much. I love him too much to be considered healthy. I know that."<br><br>"Someday, you're gonna get out of here." He utters the last of his words slowly. "And everything's going to be okay."<br><br>"Tell me what you're fighting and I'll fight with you." </i>
</blockquote><br><br>My head was just spinning for the first half of the book. I didn't know what to think. And, I'll admit though that while I did enjoy the book the whole way through, there was a point where I was just like -- <i>where is this going?? </i> Is there even a way it <i>can</i> come together?? But then it did. It totally did.<br><br>I think what makes or breaks this kind of story is whether or not the explanation at the end makes sense and genuinely answers all the questions and fills in all the blanks. And this one did make sense.<br><br>The build-up was quiet but powerful. I read this book in one sitting and the closer I got to the end, the faster I flipped the pages. I was desperate for answers. I had chills and was just holding my breath!!<br><br>In all honesty, when I finished the book, my first thought was just WOAH. Then my second thought was along the lines of -- "No way. No way that <i>actually</i> worked." But then... I went back over the story scene by scene, moment by moment and if you look at it, it all works. It really all makes sense. <br><br>I will say though that even though the ending was fully resolved, I maybe would have wanted more details <i>given</i> to me. In this case, I was basically told the answer but left to go back and figure out how all the pieces fit together for myself. On the flip side, it was kind of fun to go back and look at each scene from a different light after knowing the twist. When I was finished the book, I literally just sat there re-reading scenes as I figured out what was <i>really</i> happening in each one. It was very complex and while a part of me did kind of wish the book had kind of walked me through it a little more, the bottom line is that the book <i>does</i> have a fully resolved ending. It's crazy the way it all works out but it does.<br><br>By the way, this is not a 'dark' romance, nor is it disturbing. It's the story of a girl and the mystery of unraveling the layers of her memories. Again, the love story is a strong element in the story and a huge part of her life. The whole plot is just very complex and makes you question everything you read.<br><br>I really love it when a book is able to genuinely take me by surprise and keep me guessing like this one did. The more I think about all the layers, the more impressed I am with the way it all came together. I loved that the book leaves you <i>thinking</i>. I'm still running sections of it over and over in my mind processing it from all the different angles. It's really very well done!<br><br>If you're looking for a really <i>different</i> read that'll mess with your mind and take you on a crazy ride, try this one out! It was SO good!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"He holds me and I know I'm safe."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><b> Rating: 4.5 stars. This is a standalone. </b><br><br>****************************<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, book news and updates:<br>✦ <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Main blog: Aestas Book Blog</a><br>✦ <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook Blog Page</a><br>✦ <a href="https://twitter.com/AestasBookBlog" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> <br><br><a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380306821i/688100._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="14492222246465742596" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_476432051" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/476432051" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/476432051?book_show_action=true">Oct 22, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it

<span id="freeTextContainer14603801552648985392"><b>3.5 stars!</b> <br/><br/><i>Unravel</i> has one of the most gorgeous covers and an intriguing blurb. I've wanted to read this book for so long, but for some reason or another, I put it off. When I started reading, I was hooked. For some reason though, as the story went on, I got distracted. I'm not sure if it was the narration of the audiobook, or my mind set, but I never got fully invested in it.   <span id="freeText14603801552648985392" style="display:none"><b>3.5 stars!</b> <br /><br /><i>Unravel</i> has one of the most gorgeous covers and an intriguing blurb. I've wanted to read this book for so long, but for some reason or another, I put it off. When I started reading, I was hooked. For some reason though, as the story went on, I got distracted. I'm not sure if it was the narration of the audiobook, or my mind set, but I never got fully invested in it. There were two big twists, and although one I guessed early one, one surprised me- although due to what I may have missed zoning out, I didn't quite understand it. Either way, this is one of those books I wished I would have READ instead of listened to. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17878481626301410624"><b>4.5 Stars </b><br/><br/><br/><span>[image error]</span><br/><br/>This story brings a reader on a journey into Naomi Carradine’s mind. Naomi is a patient at FairFax Mental Institution for the past two months. She starts to open up to her new doctor and so her story begins... <br/><br/><b>
  <i>”Listen closely. Hang onto every word. But most of all, please believe me.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>Naomi takes a reader through her past, while her new doctor tries to help her find out the truth without destroying her. <br/><br/>There is a great cast of characters, Lachlan, Max and Lana who all </span>
  <span id="freeText17878481626301410624" style="display:none"><b>4.5 Stars </b><br><br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>This story brings a reader on a journey into Naomi Carradine’s mind. Naomi is a patient at FairFax Mental Institution for the past two months. She starts to open up to her new doctor and so her story begins... <br><br><b>
  <i>”Listen closely. Hang onto every word. But most of all, please believe me.”</i>
</b><br><br>Naomi takes a reader through her past, while her new doctor tries to help her find out the truth without destroying her. <br><br>There is a great cast of characters, Lachlan, Max and Lana who all hold a piece to Naomi’s sanity as well as a keys to her freedom.<br><br><b>
  <i>”Remember me. I’m real.”</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <i>”Tell me what your fighting and I’ll fight with you,” he whispered into my hair.”</i>
</b><br><br>I loved the writing and although most readers could predict the course of events, (the author was very generous with clues, perhaps too generous) it still was one hell of a journey. I had a lot of fun drawing my conclusions while approaching Naomi’s reality and would definitely recommend this book.<br><br><b><i>”God offers to every mind it’s choice between truth and repose. Take which you please – you can never have both.” </i> </b></span>

<div id="review_724803713" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/724803713" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/724803713?book_show_action=true">Sep 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=abused-heroine">abused-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=dark-angsty">dark-angsty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=cover-lust-i-has-it">cover-lust-i-has-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer724803713" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11124839808056476861"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414614193i/11670931._SX540_.jpg' alt=' photo Unravelquotey_zps43fe3ecd.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Wow! This was such an incredible read! Never have I been more entranced by a book when I really didn’t have a clear picture of what was actually going on. This is one of those books that’s really hard to review – there’s so much I want to say but, more than anything, I absolutely don’t want to spoil this one for anyone. The mysterious blurb really isn’t giving much away and I went into this blind, not knowing what to expect and I sincerely believe that is how to get the very most out of this boo</span>
  <span id="freeText11124839808056476861" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414614193i/11670931._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo Unravelquotey_zps43fe3ecd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Wow! This was such an incredible read! Never have I been more entranced by a book when I really didn’t have a clear picture of what was actually going on. This is one of those books that’s really hard to review – there’s so much I want to say but, more than anything, I absolutely don’t want to spoil this one for anyone. The mysterious blurb really isn’t giving much away and I went into this blind, not knowing what to expect and I sincerely believe that is how to get the very most out of this book and that’s how I want you all to go in. I want you to all get the WOW factor when you read it. I promise that this is a spoiler-free review.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392801430i/8613630._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo unravelquote_zps591c9a44.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As the blurb says we know Naomi has been admitted to a pscyh ward and we know there are two important men in her life – Lachlan and Max. Naomi is tortured by visions, memories and the past and her story is slowly revealed throughout the book, mostly as her recollections to her new shrink. It’s all smoke and mirrors and the truth is shrouded in mist that only very slowly clears. I thought I had it figured out a couple of times but I was wrong and even when I did guess the secret at the heart of the story, and that was at about 90%, I still didn’t work out the whole of it.<br><br><br><blockquote>Most people believe the truth is a delicate little bird. They think it’s harmless.<br><br>But I know something they don’t.<br><br>If they dare to move their hands away from their body, they’ll discover that the little bird is gone. It’s torn their skin apart, traveled to the core of their souls, right where it hurts the most.<br><br>And that’s why I’m here and they aren’t.</blockquote><br><br>This was so beautifully written, such a well-crafted and meticulously thought out plot that I found myself turning the pages long into the wee small hours. I just had to know where it was all leading. Naomi has significant people in her life but you’re never sure as you read the book what is actually real and what is actually a fabrication of Naomi’s disturbed mind. The people that have surrounded Naomi are, for the most part, characters that I really learnt to love and I so wanted them all to be real but their stories just don’t ‘fit’ and I struggled for the longest time to make sense of what was really happening but I was utterly compelled and so incredibly intrigued.<br><br>I actually found some scenes really quite frightening. Despite being surrounded by people who want to help her, I got very strongly a deep sense of loneliness and isolation from Naomi. People want to reach out and help her but she’s got to really ‘see’ things first for that mist to clear for her to become well and to accept their help. There is, of course, a villain and when Naomi’s tortured mind conjures him up when she’s alone in her room at the psych hospital, I felt and overwhelming sense of malevolence and keenly felt her terror.<br><br><blockquote>I hear his voice. It’s gritty. It’s harsh. It makes my blood freeze in my veins.<br><br>“Are you afraid of me?” he asks<br><br>Sweat beads on my upper lip as I stare down at my legs.<br><br>Don’t you speak to him. Don’t you dare, I tell myself.<br><br>I look up.<br><br>He crouches down. I hear his joints pop from the movement. It sounds like thunder. It ricochets in my skull until I grip the sides of my head in pain to make it stop.<br><br>He’s the one that speaks to me. He’s the one that terrifies me. He’s the very core of my nightmares.</blockquote><br><br>This was so powerfully delivered that it built up to such an incredible crescendo and I was truly taken aback when, eventually, everything became clear. As a blogger, I read a lot of books and very few have the power to truly surprise me but this one definitely did. It’s a genuinely different read, one that’s very difficult to put down. It’s a very much a romance but I was so conflicted as I read it – both men in her life are just wonderful, the genuine love, affection and chemistry that they share really does leap off the page but you’re never sure what’s real and what isn’t.<br><br><br>When you finish the book, you will realise that all the clues are there and it’s the kind of ending that will make want to turn straight back to page one and read again, with full disclosure, knowing everything and really look at the story one more time.<br><br>I think this has just about everything – romance, intrigue, suspense, sex and a fair sized serving of despair. It’s a book that’s going to stay with me for a very long time, it’s really quite unforgettable. It’s at once disturbing and hopeful and I can highly recommend it. There’s very little I can say about the plot without giving too much away and I so don’t want to do that so all I can say is – this isn’t a book that you just read, this is a book that you experience. You just have to go with the confusing flow and let the story slowly unravel in front of you right through to the stunning reveal at the end.<br><br><br> <br><br>5 stunning stars<br><br>5 stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="11124839808056476861" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1535355821" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1535355821" />
    <a title="warhawke" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke"><img alt="warhawke" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431835527p2/25494927.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1535355821?book_show_action=true">Feb 02, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="warhawke" class="user" itemprop="url" name="warhawke" href="/user/show/25494927-warhawke">warhawke</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=mystery-suspense-horror">mystery-suspense-horror</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25494927-warhawke?shelf=romance-love">romance-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1535355821" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer18212334980797053474"><b>Genre: </b>Psychological Thriller/Romantic Suspense<br/><b>Type: </b>Standalone Book 1 of Fairfax series<br/><b>POV: </b> First Person - Female<br/><b>Rating: </b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454233754i/17933279.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454602120i/17990418.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Naomi Carradine was a college student from a respectable family. While on summer break with her best friend Lana, a life-changing event led to her stay at Fairfax Mental Health Institute. Confused and alone, she was determined to find her way out back into her world with only one person who always had her back.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453882133i/17883711.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>The human mind is such a fascinating thing and that’s why I’ve a</span>
  <span id="freeText18212334980797053474" style="display:none"><b>Genre: </b>Psychological Thriller/Romantic Suspense<br><b>Type: </b>Standalone Book 1 of Fairfax series<br><b>POV: </b> First Person - Female<br><b>Rating: </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454233754i/17933279.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454602120i/17990418.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Naomi Carradine was a college student from a respectable family. While on summer break with her best friend Lana, a life-changing event led to her stay at Fairfax Mental Health Institute. Confused and alone, she was determined to find her way out back into her world with only one person who always had her back.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453882133i/17883711.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The human mind is such a fascinating thing and that’s why I’ve always been attracted to stories related to it. I’m happy that this book certainly met my needs.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>I can dream. I can imagine and hope, but it will never change a thing.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>I love taking the journey with Naomi through her ups and downs, and her confusion and revelation. I also love seeing her interaction with the people around her at the institution. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>My opinion matters to him. And even as a kid it had mattered. That’s what makes Lachlan my safety net—I will always matter to him.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>Lachlan was a highly likeable character. His unwavering support gave Naomi the strength to move on. I love seeing how their relationship evolved from the first time they met.<br><br>Lana and Max were another two closest people in her life. Both of them came into her circle at the right moment in her life. Each of them had individual strengths and weaknesses that helped her navigate through life. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454602229i/17990447.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Even though I managed to figure things out before the revelation it didn’t distract me from enjoying the overall story. However, I do wish I could feel more of her distress. <br><br>Unravel is a story of a woman’s struggle in unraveling the truth from the depth of her mind. It’s a good choice if you’re looking for something that touches the complexity of human minds. <br><br> <i><b>Note:</b><br>The book is not dark but there were scenes that might be disturbing to some. </i><br><br><br><b>Books in the series:</b><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16466436.Unravel__Fairfax___1_" title="Unravel (Fairfax, #1) by Calia Read" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1394658584s/16466436.jpg" alt="Unravel (Fairfax, #1) by Calia Read" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23834615.Unhinge__Fairfax___2_" title="Unhinge (Fairfax, #2) by Calia Read" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1447193185s/23834615.jpg" alt="Unhinge (Fairfax, #2) by Calia Read" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<span id="freeTextContainer17722932223266941418"><b> ***3 "WHAT THE FUCK JUST HAPPENED" STARS**</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392923627i/8634394._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>"Well, that's a whole other twist that baffled Dr. Ruthledge and the rest of the doctors."</b>........AND ME!!!! <br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392885961ra/8627815.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>If your an avid Mindfuck/ Dark reader <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16466436.Unravel' title='Unravel by Calia Read' rel='nofollow noopener'>Unravel</a> will most likely be fairly predictable.. I guessed the majority of the plot twist early on (as did most readers, so don't be too impressed by me). I was wrong about one thing ( Oh' well, I never said I was perfect).<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392923627i/8634394._SX540_.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>I liked Naomi, Lana, Max and LOVED-LOVED-LOVED Lachlan( he can light my match ANY DAY!)</span>
  <span id="freeText17722932223266941418" style="display:none"><b> ***3 "WHAT THE FUCK JUST HAPPENED" STARS**</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392923627i/8634394._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>"Well, that's a whole other twist that baffled Dr. Ruthledge and the rest of the doctors."</b>........AND ME!!!! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392885961ra/8627815.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If your an avid Mindfuck/ Dark reader <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16466436.Unravel" title="Unravel by Calia Read" rel="nofollow noopener">Unravel</a> will most likely be fairly predictable.. I guessed the majority of the plot twist early on (as did most readers, so don't be too impressed by me). I was wrong about one thing ( Oh' well, I never said I was perfect).<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1392923627i/8634394._SX540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I liked Naomi, Lana, Max and LOVED-LOVED-LOVED Lachlan( he can light my match ANY DAY!). Unfortunately the ending killed the story for me. I was left with too many questions... BUT this book has numerous 5 stars reviews. Maybe I just need further clarification..<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392885961ra/8627816.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Said questions..<b> DO NOT OPEN UNTIL YOU'VE READ THE BOOK.</b><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Will you ever learn buttercup?.. j/k  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <b><br>* MAX, MAX, MAX!!</b> WTF was the deal with his character?<br>*I get he was made up but why 10 years after the abuse started??<br>* So was Lachlan arrested?<br>* Was she screaming Max's name during sex or Lachlan?? If she was screaming Max, that should have been a huge red flag for Lachlan.<br>* What happened to her cunt of a mother?? ---&gt; hello, child neglect!<br>* How did Lachlan not know something was seriously wrong with his girlfriend? His mother surely did.<br>* Why was Dr. Ruthledge assigned Naomi, Dr. Woods admitted/ was her primary Doctor.. Whom had no desire to help her as he was helping the family cover up their dirty little secret.<br>* Did Naomi attend school or was she home schooled? I remember P.E. being mentioned. I don't think homeschool students have P.E.<br>* Too convenient of an ending.. The Doctor shows up and helps cover for Lachlan... NAH.. I'm not feeling it...Besides, Naomi should been the one to kill her father... and CUNT of a mother.... just sayin'<br>* So , did her daddy's little secret finally come out? <br>* How was Lachlan authorized visitation so frequently? <br>* Did she ever move/ have an apartment or was that a figment of her imagination?<br>* Was I the only put off by the age difference? She was 10 and he ws 15 when they first met. What 15 year old is going to spend that much time with a 10year old girl?.. when they finally bumped uglies, Naomi was 17 and Lachan was 22--&gt; Eeek! <br>* I'm sure I have a few more questions but my brain hurts so I shall shut up now..  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>....Can someone help me PLEASE?? <br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392886587ra/8627853.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Please do not let me deter you from reading <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16466436.Unravel" title="Unravel by Calia Read" rel="nofollow noopener">Unravel</a>...In fact, PLEASE read it and answer my laundry list of questions... <div id="review_1714088122" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1714088122" />
    <a title="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell"><img alt="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1584062476p2/2190064.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1714088122?book_show_action=true">May 17, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell" href="/user/show/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell">Nenia ✨️ Socially Awkward Trash Panda ✨️ Campbell</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell?shelf=pretty-cover-sparklies">pretty-cover-sparklies</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2190064-nenia-socially-awkward-trash-panda-campbell?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1714088122" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17420153548754345533"><a href='http://readasaurus.blogspot.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459070464i/18565492.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a href='https://www.instagram.com/neniagram/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Instagram</a> || <a href='https://twitter.com/NeniaCampbell' rel='nofollow noopener'>Twitter</a> || <a href='https://www.facebook.com/aficionenias/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Facebook</a> || <a href='http://www.amazon.com/Nenia-Campbell/e/B00AWVRKMS' rel='nofollow noopener'>Amazon</a> || <a href='https://www.pinterest.com/mightbeamisprin/' rel='nofollow noopener'>Pinterest</a><br/><br/><br/>I was watching a YouTube video recently about a psychiatrist talking about the portrayal of mental illness in films, and while talking about schizophrenia, he went on this side tangent about how he knew a couple patients who suffered from visual hallucinations and part of how they dealt with that was with their pets. If their cat or dog didn't react to the hallucination, then no matter how real it seemed, <i>they </i>knew it wasn't real.<br/><br/><br/><br/>I remem</span>
  <span id="freeText17420153548754345533" style="display:none"><a href="http://readasaurus.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1459070464i/18565492.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.instagram.com/neniagram/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> || <a href="https://twitter.com/NeniaCampbell" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> || <a href="https://www.facebook.com/aficionenias/" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> || <a href="http://www.amazon.com/Nenia-Campbell/e/B00AWVRKMS" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a> || <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/mightbeamisprin/" rel="nofollow noopener">Pinterest</a><br><br><br>I was watching a YouTube video recently about a psychiatrist talking about the portrayal of mental illness in films, and while talking about schizophrenia, he went on this side tangent about how he knew a couple patients who suffered from visual hallucinations and part of how they dealt with that was with their pets. If their cat or dog didn't react to the hallucination, then no matter how real it seemed, <i>they </i>knew it wasn't real.<br><br><br><br>I remembered that video while reading Calia Read's UNRAVEL. I thought to myself, "Oh, man, what Naomi needs is a dog."<br><br><br><br>UNRAVEL is an interesting new adult book. Read's style, in how she combines mind-fucks and psychology, reminds me a lot of Tarryn Fisher's. Our heroine, Naomi, is in a mental hospital. We don't know why she's there, and neither does she. All she knows is that something horrible must have happened and that she needs to get out to save her two friends, Max and Lana.<br><br><br><br>This is one of those books where saying too much about it will ruin the entire story, but it has some pretty dark themes - mental illness, obviously; abuse; rape; self-harm; suicide; and so much more. The themes fit the story, though, and don't feel like they're thrown in there for shock value. The reveal, when it comes, is chilling. I saw it coming, but I have a degree in psychology and have read about some cases that were similar to this. That's all I'm going to say.<br><br><br><br>If you're tired of the typical instalove new adult formula, UNRAVEL is a great way to break the mold. It's dark AF, and a little slow in the beginning, but I feel like it's worth the ride - especially if you enjoy Tarryn Fisher's MUD VEIN.<br><br><br><br>3 to 3.5 stars</span>
  <a data-text-id="17420153548754345533" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_483025972" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/483025972" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/483025972?book_show_action=true">Dec 22, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=emotional-rollercoaster">emotional-rollercoaster</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=unputdownable">unputdownable</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=mind-fuck">mind-fuck</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer483025972" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5329192957437294450"><br/>★★★★ <b>4 stars!</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>"Just remember that even the purest of souls have darkness in them."</i>
</blockquote><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395663466i/9026016.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Okay, I'm not going to say much about the synopsis of the book. I think the blurb says it all and saying much more might spoil the story for those who haven't read this book yet. So, here it goes:</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>Six months ago, I was happy. I was simply Naomi Carradine. <br/><br/>One month ago, I was admitted into a psych ward. <br/><br/>Yesterday, Lachlan visited me. Kissed me. And told me that I’m starting to lose my mind. <br/>Hours later, Max ha</i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText5329192957437294450" style="display:none"><br>★★★★ <b>4 stars!</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Just remember that even the purest of souls have darkness in them."</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395663466i/9026016.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Okay, I'm not going to say much about the synopsis of the book. I think the blurb says it all and saying much more might spoil the story for those who haven't read this book yet. So, here it goes:</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>Six months ago, I was happy. I was simply Naomi Carradine. <br><br>One month ago, I was admitted into a psych ward. <br><br>Yesterday, Lachlan visited me. Kissed me. And told me that I’m starting to lose my mind. <br>Hours later, Max haunted my thoughts, reminding me I’m not crazy and that he needs my help. <br><br>A few minutes ago, I drifted further from reality, trying to unravel the past. <br><br>And now...everyone thinks I’m insane. But, I know he's real, and I know he needs me. <br><br><b>Do you believe me?</b></i>
</blockquote><br><br>The blurb immediately caught my attention and made me very curious to find out what the story was all about. Unravel was an intense, emotional, passionate, heartbreaking, powerful journey told from the point of view of a girl who's desperate to tell her story and find out what really happened to her. It took me a long time to figure out what was real and what wasn't but in the end everything came together and it all made perfect sense. <br><br>The writing style was very fluent and easy to read and it kept me hooked from the very first page until the very last one. The setting of this story, being that a lot of the scenes took place in a mental hospital, reminded me a bit of the one in Insanity by Lauren Hammond but I thought that Unravel was less dark, less confusing and with a much clearer ending. Not only is this a story about self-discovery and about a girl haunted by her past, but it is also a love story and the combination of both turned out to be a perfect, thrilling mix that made me desperate to find out the truth and hope for a happy ending for Naomi Carradine, this tortured girl whose only wish is for someone to believe her...<br><br><b>Highly recommend read!</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"I'm not crazy," I repeat. "I'm not crazy. I'm not crazy..."</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1395854626i/9053145.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Tell me what you're fighting and I'll fight it with you."</i>
</blockquote><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="5329192957437294450" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

It would be the one to kill me."</i><br/><br/>I’d like to thank my dear friend Karla to recommend this incredible book to me! So, thank you so much my friend! I really enjoyed it and I loved it. It was fantastic. The story was well-paced; all the characters were perfect. The story was so exciting. I suggest if you want to read this book, go through it blind and don’t read any reviews!<br/><br/>Naomi had </span>
  <span id="freeText302471424377483531" style="display:none"><b>5 Stars</b><br /><br /><i>"F*ck the truth. It was the heart that was my worst enemy. It was the one that was going to cut me. Bleed me. It would be the one to kill me."</i><br /><br />I’d like to thank my dear friend Karla to recommend this incredible book to me! So, thank you so much my friend! I really enjoyed it and I loved it. It was fantastic. The story was well-paced; all the characters were perfect. The story was so exciting. I suggest if you want to read this book, go through it blind and don’t read any reviews!<br /><br />Naomi had been involuntarily admitted to Fairfax mental health institution for thirty days. She is there because she fell apart.<br /><br /><i>"Every day is an unknown for me. Every day I wake up feeling like I’m surrounded by a heavy fog and I know I’m missing a piece of myself, and I don’t know where it is."</i><br /><br />Naomi thinks she knows the truth but doctors have another idea. The story alternates between her past and her present life at institute. She speaks about her life in the past with a psychiatrist about Max who she is in love with him. Other than Max there is another guy, Lachlan, who was in her childhood and is in her present. He is the only source of her support.<br /><br /><i>"Even when you’re angry, love tugs at your soul in the most beautiful way. It makes you care-makes you feel-when that’s the last thing you want."</i><br /><br />Other than Max and Lachlan, there is Lana. She is her best friend. They have grown up with each other. life for Lana is like torture. And Naomi will do every thing to help her.<br /><br />Okay, I read these books and I always had guesses that were right or wrong. But in this case I couldn’t even guess because everything was so real and actually I didn’t feel some thing is wrong. I constantly questioned myself about all the characters!<br /><br /><i>"Am I really here? Sure, in the physical sense I am, but that means nothing. It’s my soul, the very core of me that feels split up. And Max, Lachlan, and Lana hold those pieces."</i><br /><br />Well, when I finished nearly half of the book I took my chance and stuck to a possibility and guess what? I was 50% right! And I am proud of myself! I said all of these to say Ms. Read’s writing is so perfect, so interesting, so mysterious, so… .</span>

  <i>"…everyone thinks I’m insane. But, I know he’s real, and I know he needs me. Do you believe me?"</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/tumblr_n0vf50mWId1qan0hfo1_250_zps1568fc9b.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392760520ra/8606396.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_n0vf50mWId1qan0hfo1_250_zps1568fc9b.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The book goes through her relationship with childhood friend/love, Lachlan, her best friend Lana, and her current love interest, Max. Some bad things happen and she tries to help. It has a cause and effect of setting other things into motion which leads her to eventually wind up in the psychiatric ward.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/677003.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Lachlan wants her better, Lana hasn’t talked to her, and Max needs her help. But she has to get un-crazy to get out and help save Max. And the only way she can do this is by figuring out the truth behind what happened. She tries to go over her story with her new doctor, Dr. Rutledge. <br><br><b>
  <i>”Fuck the truth. It was the heart that was my worst enemy. It was the one that was going to cut me. Bleed me. It would be the one to kill me.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY%202/tumblr_m46txvBPkn1rpibtso1_500_zps910ba5a2.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>OK SPOILER TIME! Do not click on link unless you want to know what happens in this book! <b>I REPEAT! DO NOT CLICK UNLESS YOU WANT TO KNOW! IF YOU CLICK AND GET MAD WELL IT’S YOUR OWN DAMN FAULT! </b> K. Thanks<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I totally figured out that Naomi was actually Lana and it was her dad that had done everything towards the beginning of the book<br>I didn’t realize that Lachlan was Max though until the end. </a><br><br><br>I don’t want to totally spoil this for those who still plan on reading it but some of my gripes were:<br><br>-How many twenty year olds actually read a physical newspaper nowadays? ANYONE? ANYONE? That’s how she found out that??? Put that shit in the online newspaper…<br><br>-Really what purpose did Dr. Rutledge play, I mean even at the end? I feel since Dr. Woods was involved how Dr. Rutledge was even assigned to care for Naomi.<br><br>- The weekend pass. What was the point…..I just don’t get it….<br><br>-Why was she put there <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ if the mom was just going to sign her out, it makes no sense to me  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>-Also <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ she was released and her mom took her home and her dad confronts her and Lachlan shows up to save her and kill's the dad and of course Dr. Rutledge shows up?  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><br><a href="http://s59.photobucket.com/user/cotejb/media/FUNNY/tumblr_lm7dl3ZRzK1qii6tmo1_400_zps75c8adc9.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer4729698132997447442"> <b>Such a weird book.</b> I have no idea how to write this review and not spoil it for you, that is why this will be a mini review. Unravel is one of those stories that is best to pick up and read. Skip book summary and other people thoughts about it. That was just what I had done.<br/><br/> Actually, you can read a book summary. It won't tell you anything - perfect example how to write synopsis. I did have certain expectations, but this turned out to be so much more. If you want to read just another new adult </span>
  <span id="freeText4729698132997447442" style="display:none"> <b>Such a weird book.</b> I have no idea how to write this review and not spoil it for you, that is why this will be a mini review. Unravel is one of those stories that is best to pick up and read. Skip book summary and other people thoughts about it. That was just what I had done.<br /><br /> Actually, you can read a book summary. It won't tell you anything - perfect example how to write synopsis. I did have certain expectations, but this turned out to be so much more. If you want to read just another new adult romance novel, this is not it. But if you are sick of predictable stories with good girls gone bad and alpha bad boys, if you need something that will keep you on the edge until the very end, Unravel by Calia Read is perfect choice for you.<br /><br /> <b>Twisted and dark</b> - you would feel as you're losing your mind along with main character, Naomi. Even when you think that you know what comes next, you would still be unsure of your own judgement. Main focus is not on the love story, but there are two men that will drive you crazy. And than there is that other... person.<br /><br /> I will finish here before I start telling you everything, but please, just read it. I promise you that Unravel is <b>something different</b>.<br /><br />Rating: 4.5 stars<br /><br />Review posted at <a href="http://jacitamati.blogspot.com/2014/03/mini-review-unravel-by-calia-read.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Ja čitam, a ti?</a><br /></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1784467273?book_show_action=true">Jan 30, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Penny" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Penny" href="/user/show/7463065-penny">Penny</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1784467273" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer17290043034143491365">It's ok, but predictable. <br/><br/>After reading so many fantastic reviews about Unravel, I was expecting something great, yet, I found the book quite disappointing.<br/><br/>I do see what the book wants to accomplish, but it it didn’t do it for me.<br/>I realized what was going on pretty much since right after the beginning. It was way too obvious, so the story turned out to be a bit long and tedios for me, there was nothing surprising or unexpected. <br/><br/> However, if you don’t figure out what is actually going on, I can s</span>
  <span id="freeText17290043034143491365" style="display:none">It's ok, but predictable. <br /><br />After reading so many fantastic reviews about Unravel, I was expecting something great, yet, I found the book quite disappointing.<br /><br />I do see what the book wants to accomplish, but it it didn’t do it for me.<br />I realized what was going on pretty much since right after the beginning. It was way too obvious, so the story turned out to be a bit long and tedios for me, there was nothing surprising or unexpected. <br /><br /> However, if you don’t figure out what is actually going on, I can see that the resolution of the story could have some impact, and the story along the way could be more interesting. This way is the only real option I see for the book achieving so many stars. Nevertheless, there were too many things that made me see it early on, so the plot lost all its appeal for me, and I lost interest in the story. There are clues nonstop along the story, so it is hard to be blind to what is the deal. Too many hints.<br /><br />I will not continue reading this series.<br /><br />P.S.: Nice cover.</span>
